<header class="post-title">
<h1 class="title">Vegetable Fritters with Garlic Herb Sauce</h1>
<div class="post-meta">
<span class="cost">$3.19 recipe / $1.06 serving</span> </div>
<p id="breadcrumbs"><span><span><a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/">Budget Bytes</a> Â» <span><a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/category/recipes/">Recipes</a> Â» <span><a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/category/recipes/side-dish/">Side Dish Recipes</a> Â» <span aria-current="page" class="breadcrumb_last">Vegetable Fritters with Garlic Herb Sauce</span></span></span></span></span></p> </header>
<div class="wprm-recipe wprm-recipe-snippet wprm-recipe-template-custom-snippets"><a class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-jump-to-recipe-shortcode wprm-block-text-normal wprm-jump-smooth-scroll wprm-recipe-jump-inline-button wprm-recipe-link-inline-button wprm-color-accent" data-recipe="48606" data-smooth-scroll="500" href="#recipe" style="color: #2a2a2a;background-color: #ffffff;border-color: #2a2a2a;border-radius: 3px;padding: 5px 8px;"><span class="wprm-recipe-icon wprm-recipe-jump-icon"><svg height="16" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g class="nc-icon-wrapper" fill="#2a2a2a"><path d="M9,2h6c0.6,0,1-0.4,1-1s-0.4-1-1-1H9C8.4,0,8,0.4,8,1S8.4,2,9,2z" data-color="color-2"></path> <path d="M16,11V5c0-0.6-0.4-1-1-1H9C8.4,4,8,4.4,8,5v6H1.9L12,23.6L22.1,11H16z" fill="#2a2a2a"></path></g></svg></span> Jump to Recipe</a><a class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-jump-inline-button wprm-recipe-link-inline-button pl-custom-btn add-grocery" data-post-id="48601" data-recipe="1" data-recipe-key="" href="javascript:void(0)" id="grocery-popup" style="border-radius: 3px;padding: 5px 8px;"><span class="fa fa-plus"></span> GROCERY LIST</a><a class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-jump-inline-button wprm-recipe-link-inline-button pl-custom-btn add-favorite" data-collection="" data-post-id="48601" href="javascript:void(0)" id="favourite-popup" style="border-radius: 3px;padding: 5px 8px;"><span class="fa fa-heart"></span> FAVORITES</a></div><span data-image-pin-it="true" id="dpsp-post-content-markup"></span><p>Weâre kind of coming full circle here, with Budget Bytes. I started this blog as a log of what I was cooking up in my kitchen with my limited budget and over the years it has grown into a massive recipe development project. But now, with limited grocery access, Iâm returning to just showcasing the things Iâm cooking up in my kitchen with what I have. These Vegetable Fritters are one of the things Iâve made while isolating at home. Itâs just a mish-mash of the vegetables I had on hand in my fridge and freezer, fried up with a simple batter, and served with a sour cream based Garlic Herb sauce. Itâs simple, delish, and a great way to use up your leftover vegetables so they donât go to waste!<span id="more-48601"></span></p>
<h2>Easy Vegetable Fritters with Garlic Herb Dip</h2>
<p><img alt="Overhead of vegetable fritters on a paper towel lined white tray, with a bowl of garlic herb dipping sauce on the side" class="alignnone wp-image-48605 size-full" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V-400x534.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V-640x854.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V-195x260.jpg 195w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-V-768x1024.jpg 768w" height="1067" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" title="Use up your leftover frozen and fresh vegetables in this easy and flavorful vegetable fritters recipe, with a side of homemade garlic herb dipping sauce! BudgetBytes.com" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Shown with the <a href="https://www.roveandswig.com/products/enamelware-tray-v190?ref=8767660&amp;variant=8139186634853" rel="nofollow sponsored noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">small enamelware tray</a> (affiliate link).</em></p>
<h3>What Vegetables Can I Add to the Fritters?</h3>
<p>Some other vegetables that would be excellent in these fritters include: cauliflower, cabbage, spinach, mushrooms, spinach, potatoes, zucchini, eggplant, and bell pepper. For really soft, high water content vegetables, like eggplant, zucchini, and frozen spinach, you probably want to sautÃ© them first to eliminate some of the excess moisture before adding to your fritters.Â </p>
<p>No matter what vegetables you plan to add to your fritters, make sure to shred them (using a large-holed cheese grater or food processor), or chop them finely so the fritters hold together better.Â </p>
<h3>Other Add-ins</h3>
<p>If you want to make these cheesy fritters, you can add some grated Parmesan (about Â¼ cup) or some shredded cheddar (Â½ cup) to the batter. Another option is to change up the seasoning. I made my vegetable fritters super simple because I actually enjoy being able to taste the individual vegetables, but you can also experiment with adding different seasonings like ranch powder, Cajun seasoning, or a basic seasoning salt like <a href="https://www.mccormickforchefs.com/products/lawrys/seasoned-salt" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Lawryâs</a>. Just make sure that if youâre adding a seasoning that already contains salt that you also reduce the salt added to the batter.</p>
<h3>How to Serve Vegetable Fritters</h3>
<p>Vegetable fritters make a great appetizer or side dish to just about any main. Iâd serve them next to something like <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/cheddar-cheeseburger-meatloaf/">meatloaf</a>, <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/sweet-and-spicy-glazed-chicken-thighs/">Glazed Chicken Thighs</a>, <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/sloppy-joes-plus/">Sloppy Joes</a>, <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/marinated-portobello-mushroom-burgers/">Portobello Burgers</a>, or just serve them right on top of a pile of creamy <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/fluffy-garlic-herb-mashed-potatoes/">Garlic Herb Mashed Potatoes</a> (in place of the dipping sauce)</p>
<h3>Can I Bake the Fritters?</h3>
<p>No, these will not turn out well if baked. They definitely need to be fried in oil to create the correct texture.</p>
<h3>How Are the Leftovers?</h3>
<p>As with any fried food the fritters do not stay crispy on the edges, but I still find the leftovers to be quite flavorful and delicious! As long as youâre not expecting a crispy fritter, I think theyâre quite enjoyable as leftovers. I reheated mine using a microwave, but you could also heat them in a skillet over medium-low heat until heated through.</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name wprm-block-text-bold">Vegetable Fritters with Garlic Herb Dipping Sauce</h2>
<div class="wprm-spacer"></div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary wprm-block-text-normal"><span style="display: block;">Use up your leftover frozen and fresh vegetables in this easy and flavorful vegetable fritters recipe, with a side of homemade garlic herb dipping sauce! </span></div>
<div class="wprm-spacer"></div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-meta-container wprm-recipe-tags-container wprm-recipe-details-container wprm-recipe-details-container-separate wprm-block-text-normal" style=""><div class="wprm-recipe-block-container wprm-recipe-block-container-separate wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-tag-container wprm-recipe-recipe_cost-container" style=""><span class="wprm-recipe-details-label wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-tag-label wprm-recipe-recipe_cost-label">Total Cost: </span><span class="wprm-recipe-recipe_cost wprm-block-text-normal">$3.19 recipe / $1.06 serving</span></div></div>

<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-48606-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="48606"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Instructions</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group"><ul class="wprm-recipe-instructions"><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-48606-step-0-0" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Make the garlic herb dipping sauce first, so the flavors have some time to blend. In a small bowl, stir together the sour cream, dried parsley, dried oregano, dried basil, garlic powder, onion powder, salt, and pepper. Refrigerate the dip until ready to eat.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-48606-step-0-1" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Allow the broccoli and corn to thaw, or use the defrost function on a microwave thaw to them. Finely chop the broccoli. Peel and grate the carrot using a large-holed cheese grater. Slice the green onions.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-48606-step-0-2" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Add the broccoli, corn, carrots, and green onion to a large bowl. Also add the flour, eggs, garlic powder, and salt. Stir until everything is evenly combined.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-48606-step-0-3" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Heat 1 Tbsp cooking oil in a large non-stick skillet (cast iron, ceramic, or teflon) over medium heat. Once the skillet is hot and the oil is shimmering, add the vegetable fritter batter to the skillet in Â¼ cup dollops, pressing the mixture down to a flat pancake once it's in the skillet. Cook the fritters for about 3 minutes on each side, or until deep golden brown on both sides. Cook 3 or 4 fritters in the skillet at a time, adding another tablespoon of oil between batches. Transfer the cooked fritters to a paper towel lined plate.</span></div></li><li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-48606-step-0-4" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Once all the fritters are cooked, serve while still warm, with the garlic herb sauce for dipping.</span></div></li></ul></div></div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-notes-container wprm-block-text-normal"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-notes-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Notes</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-notes"><span style="display: block;">If using other vegetables, use a total of about 3.5 cups finely chopped or shredded vegetables.</span></div></div>

<h2>How to Make Vegetable Fritters â Step by Step Photos</h2>
<p><img alt="A small bowl with garlic herb dipping sauce and a small spatula" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48613" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Garlic-Herb-Dipping-Sauce-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Make the garlic herb dipping sauce first so the flavors have a little time to blend. This is basically just sour cream plus my <a href="https://www.budgetbytes.com/all-purpose-garlic-herb-seasoning/">All-Purpose Garlic Herb Seasoning</a> (a half batch). It also makes a great chip dip! Stir together Â½ cup sour cream, Â½ tsp dried parsley, Â¼ tsp dried oregano, Â¼ tsp dried basil, â tsp garlic powder, â tsp onion powder, â tsp salt, and â tsp pepper. Refrigerate the dip until ready to serve.</em></p>
<p><img alt="Chopped thawed frozen broccoli florets" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48614" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Chopped-Broccoli-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Thaw Â½ lb. frozen broccoli florets and 1 cup frozen corn. Finely chop the broccoli florets.</em></p>
<p><img alt="Shredded carrot with cheese grater" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48611" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Shredded-Carrots-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Peel and shred one carrot (about 1 cup once shredded). Slice 3 green onions.</em></p>
<p><img alt="Prepared vegetables in a large bowl" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48609" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetables-in-a-Bowl-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Add the broccoli, carrot, corn, and green onion to a large bowl.</em></p>
<p><img alt="Vegetables in the bowl with flour, eggs, and seasoning." class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48615" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Flour-Eggs-and-Seasoning-added-to-vegetables-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Also add 2 large eggs, 1/2 cup all-purpose flour, 1 tsp salt, and Â¼ tsp garlic powder.</em>Â </p>
<p><img alt="Vegetable fritter batter in the bowl" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48608" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritter-Batter-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Stir until everything is evenly combined and coated in batter.</em></p>
<p><img alt="Cooked fritters in a skillet" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-48610" data-loading="lazy" data-pin-media="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan.jpg" data-src="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan.jpg 800w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-400x300.jpg 400w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-640x480.jpg 640w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-347x260.jpg 347w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-115x86.jpg 115w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-693x520.jpg 693w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-391x293.jpg 391w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-227x170.jpg 227w, https://www.budgetbytes.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Vegetable-Fritters-in-Frying-Pan-500x375.jpg 500w" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAP///wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" width="800"/></p>
<p><em>Cook the fritters in batches of 3 to 4 at a time, in a non-stick skillet (any type of non-stick, like cast iron, ceramic, or teflon). Add 1 Tbsp cooking oil to the skillet before each batch and heat over medium until the skillet is hot and the oil shimmering. Once hot, add the batter, Â¼ cup at a time, pressing it down into a pancake once itâs in the skillet. Cook for about 3 minutes on each side or until deeply golden brown.</em></p>

<p><em>Transfer the cooked vegetable fritters to a paper towel lined plate before cooking the next batch.</em></p>
